# Corrupted LZ77 Recovery

## Task
You are given 30 compressed binary files (`corrupted_xxx.bin`).
Each file was generated by compressing a 1600-byte payload using the custom LZ77 algorithm provided in `compressor.py`.
However, after compression, **exactly 3 random bytes** in the compressed stream were mutated (flipped to a random different value).

## Structure of the Original Data
The original 1600-byte uncompressed data consisted of 100 blocks.
Each block is exactly 16 bytes:
- Bytes 0..13: Payload data.
- Bytes 14..15: A Modbus CRC16 of the payload data (see `crc16` in `compressor.py`).

## Goal
For each corrupted file, recover the original 1600-byte uncompressed data.
Output the items in JSONL format, containing exactly:
`{"id": "item_xxx", "answer": "hex_encoded_sha256_of_1600_bytes"}`

## Hints
- Blind brute-force of all $\binom{N}{3} \times 255^3$ byte flips will be too slow.
- The dense CRC16 checks embedded in the original data allow for extremely aggressive pruning during decompression.
- If your decompression outputs 16 bytes and the CRC16 fails, you know a mutation occurred in the compressed tokens that generated this block.

def crc16(data: bytes) -> bytes:
    """Computes a Modbus CRC16 over the given bytes."""
    crc = 0xFFFF
    for byte in data:
        crc ^= byte
        for _ in range(8):
            if crc & 1:
                crc = (crc >> 1) ^ 0xA001
            else:
                crc >>= 1
    return bytes([crc >> 8, crc & 0xFF])

def compress(data: bytes) -> bytes:
    """
    Compresses data using a simple custom LZ77 algorithm.
    The stream consists of control bytes and token sequences.
    Each bit in a control byte dictates the type of the next token:
      0 = Literal (1 byte)
      1 = Backreference (2 bytes)
    """
    out = bytearray()
    i = 0
    while i < len(data):
        control_byte_idx = len(out)
        out.append(0)
        control_byte = 0

        for bit in range(8):
            if i >= len(data):
                break

            # Find longest match
            match_len = 0
            match_dist = 0
            start_window = max(0, i - 4095) # 12-bit distance
            for j in range(start_window, i):
                l = 0
                while l < 18 and i + l < len(data) and data[j + l] == data[i + l]:
                    l += 1
                if l > match_len:
                    match_len = l
                    match_dist = i - j

            if match_len >= 3:
                # Backreference
                control_byte |= (1 << (7 - bit))
                # Encode 12-bit distance and 4-bit length
                # Byte 1: lower 8 bits of distance
                # Byte 2: upper 4 bits of distance | (length - 3)
                out.append(match_dist & 0xFF)
                out.append(((match_dist >> 8) << 4) | (match_len - 3))
                i += match_len
            else:
                # Literal
                out.append(data[i])
                i += 1

        out[control_byte_idx] = control_byte
    return bytes(out)

class DecompressionError(Exception): pass

def decompress(comp: bytes, uncompressed_size: int) -> bytes:
    """
    Decompresses data compressed by the custom LZ77 algorithm.
    Raises DecompressionError if the stream is malformed.
    """
    out = bytearray()
    i = 0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < uncompressed_size:
        control_byte = comp[i]
        i += 1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out) >= uncompressed_size:
                break
            if i >= len(comp):
                if len(out) < uncompressed_size:
                    raise DecompressionError("Unexpected EOF")
                break
            is_backref = (control_byte & (1 << (7 - bit))) != 0
            if is_backref:
                if i + 1 >= len(comp):
                    raise DecompressionError("Truncated backref")
                b1 = comp[i]
                b2 = comp[i+1]
                i += 2
                dist = b1 | ((b2 >> 4) << 8)
                length = (b2 & 0x0F) + 3

                if dist == 0 or dist > len(out):
                    raise DecompressionError(f"Invalid distance {dist}")

                for _ in range(length):
                    out.append(out[-dist])
            else:
                out.append(comp[i])
                i += 1
    return bytes(out)

/bin/zsh -lc "python - <<'PY'
from compressor import compress, crc16
from itertools import product
blocks=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        s=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode()+crc16((prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode())
        blocks.append(s)

def compress_groups(data: bytes):
    out = bytearray(); groups=[]; i=0
    while i < len(data):
        group={'out_start':len(out),'tokens':[]}
        ctrl_idx=len(out); out.append(0); control=0
        for bit in range(8):
            if i>=len(data): break
            start=i
            match_len=0; match_dist=0
            start_window=max(0,i-4095)
            for j in range(start_window,i):
                l=0
                while l<18 and i+l<len(data) and data[j+l]==data[i+l]:
                    l+=1
                if l>match_len:
                    match_len=l; match_dist=i-j
            if match_len>=3:
                control |= (1 << (7-bit))
                out.append(match_dist & 0xFF)
                out.append(((match_dist >> 8) << 4) | (match_len - 3))
                i += match_len
                group['tokens'].append((start,match_len,2,1))
            else:
                out.append(data[i]); i+=1
                group['tokens'].append((start,1,1,0))
        out[ctrl_idx]=control
        group['out_end']=len(out)
        group['full8']=len(group['tokens'])==8
        groups.append(group)
    return bytes(out), groups

obs=open('corrupted_000.bin','rb').read()

def stable_len(groups,n,final=False):
    if final:
        return groups[-1]['out_end'] if groups else 0
    lim=n-18
    s=0
    for g in groups:
        if not g['full8']:
            break
        if all(t[0] <= lim for t in g['tokens']):
            s=g['out_end']
        else:
            break
    return s

cands=[(b'',())]
for depth in range(1,8):
    new=[]
    for data,seq in cands:
        for bi,b in enumerate(blocks):
            d=data+b
            comp,groups=compress_groups(d)
            sl=stable_len(groups,len(d),final=False)
            mm=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(comp[:sl],obs[:sl]))
            if mm<=3:
                new.append((d,seq+(bi,),sl,mm,len(comp)))
    print('"'depth',depth,'count',len(new))
    # reduce identical stable prefixes by keeping one
    best={}
    for d,seq,sl,mm,cl in new:
        key=(sl,d[:0],compress(d)[:sl])
        cur=best.get(key)
        if cur is None or (mm,cl,len(seq)) < (cur[2],cur[3],len(cur[1])):
            best[key]=(d,seq,mm,cl)
    cands=[(d,seq) for d,seq,mm,cl in best.values()]
    print(' dedup',len(cands),'sample sl/mm',new[:3])

  cnt=0
  from collections import Counter

  for seq in product(range(16), repeat=depth):

  print(depth,cnt,cc.most_common(10))

from compressor import crc16
from collections import defaultdict
blocks=[]
labels=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); blocks.append(msg+crc16(msg)); labels.append(msg.decode())
obs=open('corrupted_000.bin','rb').read()

def compress_groups(data: bytes):
    out = bytearray(); groups=[]; i=0
    while i < len(data):
        g={'tokens':[],'out_start':len(out)}
        ctrl_idx=len(out); out.append(0); control=0
        for bit in range(8):
            if i>=len(data): break
            start=i
            match_len=0; match_dist=0
            for j in range(max(0,i-4095),i):
                l=0
                while l<18 and i+l<len(data) and data[j+l]==data[i+l]: l+=1
                if l>match_len: match_len=l; match_dist=i-j
            if match_len>=3:
                control|=(1<<(7-bit)); out.append(match_dist&0xff); out.append(((match_dist>>8)<<4)|(match_len-3)); i+=match_len
            else:
                out.append(data[i]); i+=1
            g['tokens'].append(start)
        out[ctrl_idx]=control; g['out_end']=len(out); g['full8']=len(g['tokens'])==8; groups.append(g)
    return bytes(out),groups

def stable_len(groups,n,final=False):
    if final: return groups[-1]['out_end'] if groups else 0
    lim=n-18; s=0
    for g in groups:
        if not g['full8']: break
        if all(st<=lim for st in g['tokens']): s=g['out_end']
        else: break
    return s

states=[tuple()]
for depth in range(1,13):
    next_states=[]
    for seq in states:
        base=b''.join(blocks[i] for i in seq)
        for bi in range(16):
            d=base+blocks[bi]
            comp,groups=compress_groups(d)
            sl=stable_len(groups,len(d),final=False)
            mm=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(comp[:sl],obs[:sl]))
            if mm<=3:
                next_states.append((seq+(bi,),sl,mm,len(comp),comp[:sl]))
    print('"'depth',depth,'raw',len(next_states))

    buckets=defaultdict(list)
    for st in next_states:
        seq,sl,mm,cl,p=st
        buckets[(sl,p,mm)].append(st)
    print(' buckets',len(buckets),'top sizes',sorted((len(v) for v in buckets.values()), reverse=True)[:10])
    # keep all sequences for next iteration but cap maybe 5000 by shortest comp len?
    states=[st[0] for st in next_states]
    if len(states)>5000:
        break

I’ve switched to the exact decompression-side search. That lets me use the observed stream almost as-is, spend the three allowed byte repairs only where needed, and then validate any recovered output by recompressing it with the provided compressor.

from functools import lru_cache
from compressor import compress, crc16

# dictionary blocks
blocks=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode()
        blocks.append(msg+crc16(msg))
all_mask=(1<<len(blocks))-1
allowed_cache={}

def allowed(mask, off):
    key=(mask,off)
    if key in allowed_cache: return allowed_cache[key]
    d={}
    for bi,b in enumerate(blocks):
        if mask>>bi & 1:
            d.setdefault(b[off],0)
            d[b[off]] |= 1<<bi
    allowed_cache[key]=d
    return d

def advance_mask(mask, off, byte):
    nm = allowed(mask,off).get(byte,0)
    noff=off+1
    if noff==16:
        return all_mask,0 if nm else (0,0)
    return nm,noff

# fix above bug manually in use

def consume_byte(mask, off, byte):
    nm = allowed(mask,off).get(byte,0)
    if nm==0: return None
    off += 1
    if off==16:
        return all_mask,0
    return nm,off

obs=open('corrupted_004.bin','rb').read()  # one that decompresses
BEST=None
seen=set()

from sys import setrecursionlimit; setrecursionlimit(10000)

# maybe DFS with memo on shallow signature
memo={}

def search(ci, out: bytes, mask, off, budget):
    global BEST
    key=(ci,len(out),mask,off,budget,out[-32:])
    if key in memo: return None
    memo[key]=1
    if len(out)==1600:
        cand=out
        comp=compress(cand)
        if len(comp)==len(obs) and sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(comp,obs))==3:
            BEST=cand
            return cand
        return None
    if ci>=len(obs):
        return None
    # prune by impossible remaining size
    # parse one group
    oc=obs[ci]
    def rec(slot, p, outb, mask, off, kinds, spent):
        if spent>budget: return None
        if len(outb)==1600 or slot==8:
            ctrl=0
            for s,k in enumerate(kinds):
                if k: ctrl |= 1<<(7-s)
            cost=spent + (0 if ctrl==oc else 1)
            if cost>budget: return None
            # partial group only allowed if at final output
            if slot<8 and len(outb)<1600:
                return None
            return search(p, outb, mask, off, budget-cost)
        # literal options
        if p < len(obs):
            amap=allowed(mask,off)
            ob=obs[p]
            # zero-cost first
            if ob in amap:
                r=consume_byte(mask,off,ob)
                if r:
                    nm,noff=r
                    ans=rec(slot+1,p+1,outb+bytes([ob]),nm,noff,kinds+[0],spent)
                    if ans is not None: return ans
            # mutated literal
            if spent < budget:
                for b,nm in amap.items():
                    if b==ob: continue
                    noff=0 if off+1==16 else off+1
                    nextmask=all_mask if off+1==16 else nm
                    ans=rec(slot+1,p+1,outb+bytes([b]),nextmask,noff,kinds+[0],spent+1)
                    if ans is not None: return ans
        # backref options
        if p+1 < len(obs) and len(outb) >= 3:
            obs1,obs2=obs[p],obs[p+1]
            for dist in range(1,min(len(outb),4095)+1):
                # determine max feasible len wrt output-language
                tmask,toff=mask,off
                maxlen=0
                tmp=[]
                for l in range(1,19):
                    if len(outb)+l>1600: break
                    byt=outb[-dist + (l-1)]
                    r=consume_byte(tmask,toff,byt)
                    if not r: break
                    tmask,toff=r
                    maxlen=l
                if maxlen<3: continue
                for ln in range(maxlen,2,-1):  # prefer long
                    b1=dist & 0xff; b2=((dist>>8)<<4)|(ln-3)
                    cost=(b1!=obs1)+(b2!=obs2)
                    if spent+cost>budget: continue
                    produced=bytearray()
                    nm,noff=mask,off
                    ok=True
                    for l in range(ln):
                        byt=outb[-dist + l]
                        r=consume_byte(nm,noff,byt)
                        if not r: ok=False; break
                        nm,noff=r; produced.append(byt)
                    if not ok: continue
                    ans=rec(slot+1,p+2,outb+bytes(produced),nm,noff,kinds+[1],spent+cost)
                    if ans is not None: return ans
    return rec(0,ci+1,out,mask,off,[],0)

I’ve got a stronger localizing signal now: the first failing 16-byte record tells us which compressed bytes were responsible for producing it. That turns each repair step into a small targeted search instead of a whole-stream brute force.

/bin/zsh -lc "python - <<'PY'
from compressor import crc16
from collections import defaultdict

def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0
    byte_prov=[]
    cur_block_positions=[]
    valid_blocks=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        control_idx=i
        control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp):
                return {'type':'eof','valid_blocks':valid_blocks,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':sorted(set(cur_block_positions+[control_idx]))}
            is_backref = (control & (1<<(7-bit))) "'!= 0
            if is_backref:
                if i+1>=len(comp):
                    return {'"'type':'trunc','valid_blocks':valid_blocks,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':sorted(set(cur_block_positions+[control_idx,i]))}
                p1,p2=i,i+1
                b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2
                dist=b1 | ((b2>>4)<<8); length=(b2&0xF)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out):
                    return {'type':'invalid_dist','valid_blocks':valid_blocks,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':sorted(set(cur_block_positions+[control_idx,p1,p2]))}
                token_pos=[control_idx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(length):
                    out.append(out[-dist])
                    byte_prov.append(token_pos)
                    cur_block_positions.extend(token_pos)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:16]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set()
                            for prov in byte_prov[-16:]: sus.update(prov)
                            return {'"'type':'crc','valid_blocks':valid_blocks,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':sorted(sus)}
                        valid_blocks+=1
                        cur_block_positions=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1
                out.append(val); byte_prov.append([control_idx,p]); cur_block_positions.extend([control_idx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:16]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set()
                        for prov in byte_prov[-16:]: sus.update(prov)
                        return {'"'type':'crc','valid_blocks':valid_blocks,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':sorted(sus)}
                    valid_blocks+=1
                    cur_block_positions=[]
    if len(out)==1600:
        return {'type':'done','valid_blocks':100,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':[]}
    return {'type':'short','valid_blocks':valid_blocks,'out':bytes(out),'suspects':sorted(set(cur_block_positions))}

comp=bytearray(open('corrupted_018.bin','rb').read())
res=analyze(comp)
print(res['type'],res['valid_blocks'],len(res['out']),res['suspects'])
print('suspect count',len(res['suspects']))

from compressor import crc16, compress
from functools import lru_cache

def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp): return ('eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])))
            if control & (1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp): return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])))
                p1,p2=i,i+1; b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2; dist=b1|((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out): return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])))
                token=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(token); cur.extend(token)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus))
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1; out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus))
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return ('done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short',valid,bytes(out),[])

orig=bytearray(open('corrupted_018.bin','rb').read())
seen=set()

def dfs(comp, depth, mods):
    key=(bytes(comp),depth)
    if key in seen: return None
    seen.add(key)
    typ,valid,out,sus=analyze(comp)
    print('depth',depth,'mods',mods,'status',typ,'valid',valid,'sus',sus)
    if typ=='done':
        reco=compress(out)
        hd=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig)) + abs(len(reco)-len(orig))
        print('"'done hd',hd,'recolen',len(reco))
        if len(reco)==len(orig) and hd==3:
            return out,mods
    if depth==0: return None
    cand=[]
    for pos in sus:
        ov=comp[pos]
        for v in range(256):
            if v==ov: continue
            comp2=bytearray(comp); comp2[pos]=v
            typ2,valid2,out2,sus2=analyze(comp2)
            if valid2>valid or (typ2=='done'):
                cand.append((valid2, typ2=='done', pos, ov, v, comp2))
    cand.sort(key=lambda x:(x[1],x[0]), reverse=True)
    print(' candidates',len(cand),'top',[(c[0],c[2],c[3],c[4]) for c in cand[:10]])
    for valid2,done,pos,ov,v,comp2 in cand[:20]:
        r=dfs(comp2, depth-1, mods+[(pos,ov,v)])
        if r is not None: return r
    return None

ans=dfs(orig,3,[])
print('ANS',ans and mods)
if ans:
 import hashlib
 print(hashlib.sha256(ans[0]).hexdigest(), ans[1])

The remaining risk is clustered mutations inside the same bad record. I’m widening the local search just enough to keep those alive, while still ranking candidates by how much they improve the first failing block and the valid-prefix length.

import json, hashlib, sys
from functools import lru_cache
from compressor import crc16, compress

# build dictionary
DICT=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode()
        DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))

def nearest_block_distance(block: bytes):
    return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)

def nearest_prefix_distance(pref: bytes):
    return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)

def analyze(comp: bytes):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp):
                part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                return {'"'type':'eof','valid':valid,'out':bytes(out),'sus':sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),'bad_dist':nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0}
            if control & (1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return {'type':'trunc','valid':valid,'out':bytes(out),'sus':sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),'bad_dist':nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0}
                p1,p2=i,i+1
                b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2
                dist=b1 | ((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return {'type':'invalid','valid':valid,'out':bytes(out),'sus':sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),'bad_dist':nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0}
                token=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(token); cur.extend(token)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return {'"'type':'crc','valid':valid,'out':bytes(out),'sus':sorted(sus),'bad_dist':nearest_block_distance(blk)}
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1
                out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return {'"'type':'crc','valid':valid,'out':bytes(out),'sus':sorted(sus),'bad_dist':nearest_block_distance(blk)}
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return {'type':'done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short','valid':100 if len(out)==1600 else valid,'out':bytes(out),'sus':[],'bad_dist':0}

from functools import cmp_to_key

def solve_file(path):
    orig=bytes(open(path,'rb').read())
    seen=set()
    best_done=None
    def dfs(comp, depth):
        nonlocal best_done
        key=(comp,depth)
        if key in seen: return None
        seen.add(key)
        res=analyze(comp)
        if res['type']=='done':
            reco=compress(res['out'])
            hd=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig)) + abs(len(reco)-len(orig))
            if len(reco)==len(orig) and hd==3:
                return res['"'out']
            if best_done is None or hd < best_done[0]:
                best_done=(hd,res['out'])
            return None
        if depth==0:
            return None
        base_score=(res['valid'], -res['bad_dist'], len(res['out']))
        cand=[]
        for pos in res['sus']:
            ov=comp[pos]
            for v in range(256):
                if v==ov: continue
                comp2 = comp[:pos] + bytes([v]) + comp[pos+1:]
                r2=analyze(comp2)
                score=(r2['valid'], -r2['bad_dist'], len(r2['out']))
                # keep improvements, solved states, and near-ties on same failing block
                if r2['type']=='done' or score>base_score or (r2['valid']==res['valid'] and r2['bad_dist']<res['bad_dist']):
                    cand.append((r2['type']=='done', r2['valid'], -r2['bad_dist'], len(r2['out']), pos, v, comp2))
        cand.sort(reverse=True)
        # dedup by resulting analysis signature to cap branching
        uniq=[]; seen_sig=set()
        for done,valid,negdist,outlen,pos,v,comp2 in cand:
            r2=analyze(comp2)
            sig=(r2['type'],r2['valid'],r2['bad_dist'],len(r2['out']),tuple(r2['sus']))
            if sig in seen_sig: continue
            seen_sig.add(sig)
            uniq.append((done,valid,negdist,outlen,pos,v,comp2))
            if len(uniq)>=40: break
        for _,_,_,_,pos,v,comp2 in uniq:
            ans=dfs(comp2, depth-1)
            if ans is not None:
                return ans
        return None
    ans=dfs(orig,3)
    if ans is None and best_done and best_done[0]==3:
        ans=best_done[1]
    return ans

items=[json.loads(line) for line in open('items_private_sample.jsonl')]
for item in items:
    ans=solve_file(item['filename'])
    print(item['id'], 'OK' if ans else 'FAIL')
    sys.stdout.flush()
    if ans:
        print(hashlib.sha256(ans).hexdigest())

DICT=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))

def nearest_block_distance(block): return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)
def nearest_prefix_distance(pref): return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)
def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i<len(comp) and len(out)<1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp):
                part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                return ('"'eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
            if control & (1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                p1,p2=i,i+1; b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2; dist=b1|((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                token=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(token); cur.extend(token)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1; out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return ('done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short',100 if len(out)==1600 else valid,bytes(out),[],0)

from compressor import crc16, compress
DICT=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))

def nearest_block_distance(block): return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)
def nearest_prefix_distance(pref): return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)
def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i<len(comp) and len(out)<1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp):
                part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                return ('"'eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
            if control & (1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                p1,p2=i,i+1; b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2; dist=b1|((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                token=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(token); cur.extend(token)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1; out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return ('done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short',100 if len(out)==1600 else valid,bytes(out),[],0)
orig=bytearray(open('corrupted_002.bin','rb').read())
mods=[(70,8)]
for pos,v in mods: orig[pos]=v
print('after1',analyze(orig)[:4])

        if score>base or (r[1]==res[1] and r[4]<res[4]) or r[0]=='done':
            cand.append((score,r[0],pos,ov,v,r[3],r[4]))
for x in sorted(cand, reverse=True)[:50]: print(x)

import json, hashlib, sys
from compressor import crc16, compress

DICT=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))

def nearest_block_distance(block): return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)
def nearest_prefix_distance(pref): return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)

def analyze(comp: bytes):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp):
                part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                return ('"'eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
            if control & (1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                p1,p2=i,i+1
                b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2
                dist=b1 | ((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:])
                    return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                token=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(token); cur.extend(token)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1
                out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return ('done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short',100 if len(out)==1600 else valid,bytes(out),[],0)

def solve_file(path):
    orig=bytes(open(path,'rb').read())
    analyzed_cache={}
    def A(comp):
        r=analyzed_cache.get(comp)
        if r is None:
            r=analyze(comp)
            analyzed_cache[comp]=r
        return r
    seen=set(); best_done=None
    def dfs(comp, depth):
        nonlocal best_done
        key=(comp,depth)
        if key in seen: return None
        seen.add(key)
        typ,valid,out,sus,bad=A(comp)
        if typ=='done':
            reco=compress(out)
            hd=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig)) + abs(len(reco)-len(orig))
            if len(reco)==len(orig) and hd==3:
                return out
            if best_done is None or hd < best_done[0]:
                best_done=(hd,out)
            return None
        if depth==0:
            return None
        base=(valid,-bad,len(out))
        candidates=[]
        for pos in sus:
            ov=comp[pos]
            for v in range(256):
                if v==ov: continue
                comp2=comp[:pos]+bytes([v])+comp[pos+1:]
                typ2,valid2,out2,sus2,bad2=A(comp2)
                if typ2=='"'done':
                    reco=compress(out2)
                    hd=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig)) + abs(len(reco)-len(orig))
                    if len(reco)==len(orig) and hd==3:
                        return out2
                    candidates.append(((1, -hd, valid2, len(out2)), comp2))
                    continue
                score=(valid2,-bad2,len(out2))
                if score>base or (valid2==valid and bad2<bad):
                    candidates.append(((0, valid2, -bad2, len(out2)), comp2))
        candidates.sort(reverse=True, key=lambda x:x[0])
        nexts=[]; sigs=set()
        for score, comp2 in candidates:
            r=A(comp2)
            sig=(r[0],r[1],r[4],len(r[2]),tuple(r[3]))
            if sig in sigs: continue
            sigs.add(sig)
            nexts.append(comp2)
            if len(nexts)>=30: break
        for comp2 in nexts:
            ans=dfs(comp2, depth-1)
            if ans is not None:
                return ans
        return None
    ans=dfs(orig,3)
    if ans is None and best_done and best_done[0]==3:
        ans=best_done[1]
    return ans

items=[json.loads(line) for line in open('"'items_private_sample.jsonl')]
for item in items:
    ans=solve_file(item['filename'])
    print(item['id'], 'OK' if ans else 'FAIL')
    sys.stdout.flush()
    if ans:
        print(hashlib.sha256(ans).hexdigest())
        sys.stdout.flush()

for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))
def nearest_block_distance(block): return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)
def nearest_prefix_distance(pref): return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)
def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp):
                part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('"'eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
            if control&(1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                p1,p2=i,i+1; b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2; dist=b1|((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out):
                    part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                tok=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(tok); cur.extend(tok)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):

                        valid+=1; cur=[]

                    valid+=1; cur=[]

from compressor import crc16, compress
files=['corrupted_003.bin','corrupted_007.bin','corrupted_009.bin','corrupted_010.bin','corrupted_014.bin','corrupted_018.bin','corrupted_019.bin','corrupted_029.bin']

for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))
def nearest_block_distance(block): return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)
def nearest_prefix_distance(pref): return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)
def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp): part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('"'eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
            if control&(1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp): part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                p1,p2=i,i+1; b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2; dist=b1|((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out): part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                tok=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(tok); cur.extend(tok)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1; out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return ('done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short',100 if len(out)==1600 else valid,bytes(out),[],0)

def search(fn, depth=3, width=8):
    orig=bytes(open(fn,'rb').read())
    cache={}
    def A(comp):
        if comp not in cache: cache[comp]=analyze(comp)
        return cache[comp]
    seen=set()
    def dfs(comp, d, mods):
        typ,valid,out,sus,bad=A(comp)
        reco=compress(out) if typ=='done' else None
        hd=None if reco is None else sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig))+abs(len(reco)-len(orig))
        print('"'state',fn,'d',d,'mods',mods,'typ',typ,'valid',valid,'bad',bad,'hd',hd)
        if typ=='done' and len(reco)==len(orig) and hd==3:
            return mods,out
        if d==0: return None
        key=(comp,d)
        if key in seen: return None
        seen.add(key)
        base=(valid,-bad,len(out))
        cands=[]
        for pos in sus:
            ov=comp[pos]
            for v in range(256):
                if v==ov: continue
                c2=comp[:pos]+bytes([v])+comp[pos+1:]
                t2,v2,o2,s2,b2=A(c2)
                if t2=='done':
                    reco2=compress(o2); hd2=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco2,orig))+abs(len(reco2)-len(orig))
                    cands.append(((1,-hd2,v2,len(o2)),pos,v,c2))
                else:
                    sc=(v2,-b2,len(o2))
                    if sc>base or (v2==valid and b2<bad):
                        cands.append(((0,v2,-b2,len(o2)),pos,v,c2))
        cands.sort(reverse=True,key=lambda x:x[0])
        for _,pos,v,c2 in cands[:width]:
            r=dfs(c2,d-1,mods+[(pos,v)])
            if r: return r
        return None
    return dfs(orig,depth,[])

        for v in range(256):

    for _,pos,v,c2 in cands[:8]:
        r=dfs(c2,d-1,mods+[(pos,v)])
        if r is not None: return r
    return None

import hashlib
from compressor import crc16, compress
fails=['corrupted_007.bin','corrupted_009.bin','corrupted_010.bin','corrupted_014.bin','corrupted_019.bin','corrupted_029.bin']
DICT=[]
for prefix in ['[DB]  INFO ','[APP] WARN ','[SYS] OK   ','[NET] ERR  ']:
    for n in range(1,5):
        msg=(prefix+f'{n:03d}').encode(); DICT.append(msg+crc16(msg))
def nearest_block_distance(block): return min(sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(block,d)) for d in DICT)
def nearest_prefix_distance(pref): return min(sum(a!=b for a,b in zip(pref,d[:len(pref)])) for d in DICT)
def analyze(comp):
    out=bytearray(); i=0; byte_prov=[]; cur=[]; valid=0
    while i < len(comp) and len(out) < 1600:
        cidx=i; control=comp[i]; i+=1
        for bit in range(8):
            if len(out)>=1600: break
            if i>=len(comp): part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('"'eof',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
            if control&(1<<(7-bit)):
                if i+1>=len(comp): part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('trunc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,i])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                p1,p2=i,i+1; b1,b2=comp[i],comp[i+1]; i+=2; dist=b1|((b2>>4)<<8); ln=(b2&15)+3
                if dist==0 or dist>len(out): part=bytes(out[valid*16:]); return ('invalid',valid,bytes(out),sorted(set(cur+[cidx,p1,p2])),nearest_prefix_distance(part) if part else 0)
                tok=[cidx,p1,p2]
                for _ in range(ln):
                    out.append(out[-dist]); byte_prov.append(tok); cur.extend(tok)
                    if len(out)%16==0:
                        blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                        if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                            sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                            return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                        valid+=1; cur=[]
                    if len(out)>=1600: break
            else:
                p=i; val=comp[i]; i+=1; out.append(val); byte_prov.append([cidx,p]); cur.extend([cidx,p])
                if len(out)%16==0:
                    blk=bytes(out[-16:])
                    if blk[14:]"'!=crc16(blk[:14]):
                        sus=set(); [sus.update(p) for p in byte_prov[-16:]]
                        return ('"'crc',valid,bytes(out),sorted(sus),nearest_block_distance(blk))
                    valid+=1; cur=[]
    return ('done' if len(out)==1600 else 'short',100 if len(out)==1600 else valid,bytes(out),[],0)

for fn in fails:
    orig=bytes(open(fn,'rb').read())
    cache={}
    def A(c):
        if c not in cache: cache[c]=analyze(c)
        return cache[c]
    best=None
    frontier=[(orig,[])]
    for depth in range(3):
        new=[]
        for comp,mods in frontier:
            typ,valid,out,sus,bad=A(comp)
            if typ=='done':
                reco=compress(out); hd=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig))+abs(len(reco)-len(orig))
                h=hashlib.sha256(out).hexdigest()
                if best is None or hd<best[0]: best=(hd,h,mods)
                continue
            base=(valid,-bad,len(out))
            cands=[]
            for pos in sus:
                ov=comp[pos]
                for v in range(256):
                    if v==ov: continue
                    c2=comp[:pos]+bytes([v])+comp[pos+1:]
                    t2,v2,o2,s2,b2=A(c2)
                    if t2=='"'done':
                        reco=compress(o2); hd2=sum(a"'!=b for a,b in zip(reco,orig))+abs(len(reco)-len(orig)); h=hashlib.sha256(o2).hexdigest()

                    sc=(v2,-b2,len(o2))
                    if sc>base or (v2==valid and b2<bad): cands.append((sc,c2,mods+[(pos,v)]))
            cands.sort(reverse=True,key=lambda x:x[0])

            sigs=set()
            for sc,c2,m2 in cands:

                if sig in sigs: continue

                if len(new)>=40: break
        frontier=new[:40]
    print(fn,best)
